function playannouncer(arg1)
   if game.ReplicatedStorage.wkspc.Status.MapName.Value == "The Hunt" then
      return 
   end
   if player.Settings.Announcer.Value then
      if wkspc.gametype.Value == "Bombfest" then
         if Player.PlayerGui.Announcer:FindFirstChild("Sound") then
            Player.PlayerGui.Announcer.Sound:Stop()
            Player.PlayerGui.Announcer.Sound:Destroy()
         end
         local var0 = :GetChildren()[math.random(1, :GetChildren())]
         local upval0 = Instance.new("Sound")
         upval0.SoundId = var0.Value
         if .Parent:FindFirstChild("Volume") then
            upval0.Volume = .Parent.Volume.Value
         end
         if .Parent:FindFirstChild("Radio") then
            upval0.SoundGroup = game.SoundService.Radio
         elseif .Parent:FindFirstChild("Radio2") then
            upval0.SoundGroup = game.SoundService.Radio2
         end
         upval0.Parent = Player.PlayerGui.Announcer
         upval0:Play()
         if game.Players.LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("BadgeTracker") == nil then
            local var0 = Instance.new("Folder")
            var0.Name = "BadgeTracker"
            var0.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer
         end
         if game.Players.LocalPlayer.BadgeTracker:FindFirstChild("AnnouncerComments") == nil then
            local var0 = Instance.new("IntValue")
            var0.Name = "AnnouncerComments"
            var0.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.BadgeTracker
         end
         local var1 = game
         local AnnouncerComments_v0 = var1.Players.LocalPlayer.BadgeTracker.AnnouncerComments
         AnnouncerComments_v0.Value = AnnouncerComments_v0.Value + 1
         wait()
         while upval0.IsLoaded == game do
         end
         wait()
         while upval0.IsPlaying == game do
         end
         wait()
         wait()
         if player.Settings.Subtitles.Value then
            if var0:FindFirstChild("Sub") then
               var1 = getColorForSubtitle()
               Subtitles.NewSubtitle(var0.Sub.Value, upval0.TimeLength, var1)
            end
         end
         spawn(function()
            wait(upval0.TimeLength)
            upval0:Destroy()
         end)
      end
   end
end
